## SCENE 56B — WHAT THESSALY DOES NOT WRITE DOWN

*Castle Brightholm — East Gate, Late Night*

She has been writing for three hours. You know because you checked twice and told yourself both times that you were checking the perimeter. The third time you stop pretending.

Her notebook is closed when you arrive. She was waiting. Thessaly Brightwater does not accidentally leave her notebook closed when someone she wants to talk to approaches. The pen is behind her ear. The locket is in her hand — open, for once. She closes it when she sees you looking but does not put it away.

'I wrote three versions of tonight,' she says. 'The professional one. The honest one. And the one I will not send.' She looks at you with the particular directness that means she has decided something. 'You are in the third one.'

> **ROMANCE MOMENT**
> She is showing you the version of herself that does not appear in dispatches.

> **A) 'Show me.'** (+2 ROSE, ROMANCE FLAME Thessaly) --> Scene 60
>
> **B) 'Keep it. Some things do not need to be read to be known.'** (+1 ROSE, ROMANCE FLAME Thessaly) --> Scene 60
>
> **C) 'I am glad I am in any version.' Leave her to write.** (+1 ROSE) --> Scene 60

---


## SCENE 57 — ALDRIC IN THE ARMOURY

*Castle Brightholm*

He is sharpening his sword for the third time tonight. You can tell it is the third time because the blade has the particular high shine of something worked past the point of usefulness by someone who needed something to do with their hands. He looks up when he hears you.

The armoury is quiet. Tallow candles, low. Somewhere down the corridor someone is walking fast and then stopping, then fast again — the sound of a garrison trying to be ready for something it cannot fully prepare for. After a while Aldric sets the whetstone down. 'Whatever Order claims you,' he says, 'I am glad you were here this year.'

> **ROMANCE MOMENT**
> He hands you a leather wrist guard — his, slightly worn. 'Fits better than yours,' he says. He is not looking at you.

> **CONDITIONAL — IF YOU READ SCENE 53B CHOICE B**
> If in Scene 53B you chose option B (implicating Aldric): before your choice below, turn to Scene 58B (What Aldric Did) now.

> **A) Take it. 'Thank you.' The leather is warm from his hand. You carry it out of the armoury.** (+2 ROSE, ROMANCE FLAME Aldric if Spark active) --> Scene 53_HUB
>
> **B) 'You will want it back when this is over.' 'Maybe,' he says. You leave him to his whetstone. The corridor is darker than you remembered.** (+1 ROSE, +1 SWORD) --> Scene 53_HUB

---


## SCENE 58B — WHAT ALDRIC DID

*Castle Brightholm — Storeroom, Night Before Trials*

> **CONDITIONAL DARK SCENE**
> This scene occurs if Aldric is in your party AND you chose Option B in Scene 53B (watched the suspected traitor rather than reporting).

Aldric finds you before you find him. He looks like someone who has done something and cannot undo it and has not decided yet whether he should try.

He found the officer. The one Aldous named. He followed him to the storeroom where the private correspondence was hidden. And then — Aldric does not describe this part clearly, and you do not push him — something happened. The officer is alive. He is going to stay alive. He is also, currently, unconscious, bound, and in the storeroom, and Aldric hit him harder than he meant to and then harder than that and then stopped himself and he does not know what to do with what stopping himself felt like.

He looks at you. He is not asking for absolution. He is asking whether he is still the person he thought he was. He does not know yet. He wants you to help him figure it out.

> **MORAL WEIGHT**
> Aldric did not kill him. He stopped. That matters. But he also crossed a line the Measure is very clear about. The officer is a traitor. Aldric's anger was not wrong. His method was. Both of these are true at the same time.

> **OPTIONAL ROLL:** Medicine (WIS, proficiency if trained) (+1) | WIS | DC 12
>
> **SUCCESS (roll 12+):** His knuckles are split and his breathing is slightly elevated — not from exertion but from the controlled effort of not shaking. He stopped himself mid-action. That kind of stop leaves a specific mark: not guilt about what he did but the physical memory of choosing not to continue. He is more in control of himself than he believes. Tell him this.
>
> **FAILURE (roll 1-11):** He is in distress. The specific detail of his emotional state is not readable.
>
> *No dice? Flip a coin: Heads = pass | Tails = fail*

> **A) Report everything to Caeron — the officer, Aldric's actions, all of it. Aldric faces a formal reprimand. The traitor is imprisoned. The storeroom is emptied by guards before the next bell.** (+2 CROWN. Aldric looks at you with something complicated. He would have done the same. He respects this. It still costs something.) --> Scene 53_HUB
>
> **B) Report the officer. Say Aldric found him and subdued him in the line of duty. The rest is not said. You walk back through the corridor in silence. Some silences are agreements.** (+1 SWORD — this is a lie. You will both know that. Aldric owes you one. So do you.) --> Scene 53_HUB
>
> **C) Tell Aldric: 'You stopped. That is the part that matters.' Then go wake Caeron together. The walk is long enough to mean something.** (+2 ROSE — this is the hardest choice. It does not protect either of you. It is honest.) --> Scene 53_HUB

---


## SCENE 59 — WHAT CAERON CANNOT SAY

*Castle Brightholm — Great Hall*

'I became a knight because the world requires people willing to stand in front of the bad things. I have been wondering for some time whether I am still that person.' A pause. 'You make me think that I might be.'

> **OPTIONAL ROLL:** Insight (WIS, proficiency if trained) (+1) | WIS | DC 15
>
> **SUCCESS (roll 15+):** He said 'still' — present tense. This is not a past doubt: it is active. Lord Caeron Ashvale does not know if he has what this moment requires. He told you because he trusts you with it. ROMANCE FLAME Caeron activates immediately if you respond without trying to reassure him.
>
> **FAILURE (roll 1-14):** He is speaking honestly but opaquely. The layer beneath the words is not clear.
>
> *No dice? Flip a coin: Heads = pass | Tails = fail*

> **A) 'You are.' He does not say anything else. You leave the hall. The dispatch is still on the table. The candles are burning lower.** (+2 ROSE, ROMANCE FLAME Caeron) --> Scene 53_HUB
>
> **B) 'Show me at Vogler.' He looks at you steadily. Then nods once. You leave him to his planning.** (+1 ROSE, +1 SWORD) --> Scene 53_HUB
>
> **C) Paladin: something pulls you to the south field tonight. Turn to Scene P3 (The Test) before returning.** --> Scene P3

---


## SCENE 53_HUB — THE LONG NIGHT

*Castle Brightholm — Corridors, Night After the News*

> **GATE: Track companion visits this night. Dawn does not come until you have spoken with at least three people about what is coming.**

The castle does not sleep. You hear it in the way it breathes — doors that do not close all the way, footsteps at hours when the corridors should be empty, the persistent amber glow of candles that should have been doused two hours ago. The news has changed the air itself. Two thousand soldiers. Three days. Maybe two.

You walk the corridors because standing still feels like consent to fear, and moving feels like something you can control. The people you care about are each handling this in their own way, in their own corners of the garrison. You have time. The night is long when no one is sleeping.

> **A) (If not yet visited) Go to your companions — Aldric is in the armoury, Mira is in the infirmary, Serath watches the south road.** --> Scene 54
>
> **B) (If not yet visited) Stay in the great hall. Someone else stayed too.** --> Scene 55
>
> **C) (If not yet visited) Find Thessaly. She has been writing since the briefing.** --> Scene 56
>
> **D) (If not yet visited) Find Aldric in the armoury.** --> Scene 57
>
> **E) (If not yet visited) Something is wrong about the timing. Investigate.** --> Scene 53B
>
> **F) (If not yet visited, Tariel in party) Find Tariel.** --> Scene 53D
>
> **G) (If not yet visited, Lysander in party) Find Lysander.** --> Scene 53E
>
> **H) (If not yet visited, Mira and Serath both present) The infirmary door is ajar. You hear voices inside.** --> Scene 54B
>
> **I) (If 3+ visits) The candles have burned to nothing. The sky outside is not black any more — it is the deep grey that comes before grey becomes blue. Dawn is close.** --> Scene 53_HUB_MORN
>
> **J) The alarm bell — south wall! Draconians at the breach!** (+1 SWORD) --> Scene 53_BREACH
>
> **K) Smoke from the grain stores. Not cook-fire smoke. Something is wrong.** (+1 SWORD) --> Scene 53_SABOTAGE

---


## SCENE 53_BREACH — THE WALL BREACH

*Castle Brightholm — South Wall, Deep Night*

The bell is not the sentry bell. It is the wall bell — the one you were told about in the first week, the one that means the garrison itself is under attack. It rings three times and each strike pushes the night a little further away from silence and a little closer to chaos.

The south wall has a weakness. Everyone knows about it — a section where the mortar has been crumbling since before you arrived, where the stones shift when the wind is strong. The engineers were supposed to shore it up last month. Last month, there was no Dragon Army two days south. Last month, there was time.

There is no time now. The breach is eight feet wide and the draconians are already through.

You arrive at the wall and the scene is this: torchlight, dust from the broken stone, the sound of armoured things moving fast, and Ser Aldous — the old knight, the chapel keeper, the man who taught you what the Measure means when it is not just words — standing in the breach with his sword drawn and blood on his ribs. A draconian blade found the gap in his mail. He is fighting anyway.

He will not last. You can see it in the way he favours his left side, in the way his sword arm is slowing. Two rounds, maybe three. After that, the breach is open and the garrison's south flank is exposed.

> **COMBAT MODE**
> **Pen & Paper:** Use stat blocks below. Run the encounter at your table, then skip to **AFTER THE FIGHT**.
> **Narrative Mode:** Follow the rounds below. Roll when prompted.

> **INJURED NPC — SER ALDOUS**
> Draconian blade across the ribs. Deep cut, bleeding badly. Collapses in 2 rounds without healing.
> **Heal him:** Paladin Cure Wounds (1 spell slot, heals 2d8+CHA), Paladin Lay on Hands (from pool), Mira (if present, stabilize + 1d6+2), Bandage (stabilize at 1 HP), Potion of Healing (2d4+2).
> *Record any resources spent.*
> **If healed:** Aldous survives. He presides over the Trials at dawn with full authority. +1 ROSE at the ceremony. He remembers what you did.
> **If not healed:** Aldous collapses. A different knight presides over the Trials — competent, but without Aldous's gravitas. The ceremony feels incomplete. Aldous recovers eventually, but slowly.

> **COMPANION SELECTION — 'GATHER YOUR PARTY'**
> You have seconds. Choose 2 companions. The combination changes the fight.
>
> **Aldric + Mira:** Aldric holds the breach, Mira heals Aldous. Solid. Defensive. The safe choice.
> **Aldric + Sera:** Aldric holds, Sera picks targets. Aggressive. Fast. You need to heal Aldous yourself.
> **Aldric + Lysander:** Two frontline fighters and a veteran. Devastating offence. No healer unless you are one.
> **Mira + Sera:** Healing and range. You are the only melee fighter. The breach depends on you alone.
> **Mira + Serath:** Mira heals, Serath exploits chaos. Unconventional. Effective if you are creative.
> **Sera + Serath:** Scout and shadow. No healer. No shield wall. Fast, sharp, dangerous for everyone.
> **Lysander + Mira:** Veteran muscle and healing. Lysander takes point. You support.
> *Any other combination of available companions: use their standard action options.*

> **ENEMY STAT BLOCKS (Pen & Paper)**
> **Baaz Draconian — Wave 1 (2):** AC 13, HP 18, Speed 30ft. Scimitar +4 (1d6+2). Claw +4 (1d4+2). Death Throes: turns to stone, weapon stuck (DC 11 STR to free).
> **Baaz Draconian — Wave 2 (2):** Same stats. Arrive at Round 3. Climbing through the rubble. They have been waiting for the first wave to create the opening.

---

### NARRATIVE COMBAT — ROUND 1

The breach is full of dust and noise and the particular chaos of a fight in a confined space. The two Baaz are through the wall and pressing into the courtyard — one has engaged Aldous, the other is turning toward the armoury door. If it gets past, the interior is exposed.

Torchlight catches the draconians' scales — bronze, dull, scratched from the stone they broke through. Their eyes are the worst part. Flat. Patient. The eyes of things that are doing a job and are good at it.

Aldous parries a scimitar thrust and his knees buckle. Blood is soaking through his tabard on the left side. He does not make a sound. Knights do not, apparently, even when they should.

> **YOUR ATTACK — Choose a target:**
> **Baaz engaging Aldous** / **Baaz heading for the armoury door**
>
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll | DC 13 (Baaz AC)
> Roll 1d20 + your attack bonus.
> **ON HIT:** Roll damage.

> **COMPANION ACTION — Choose one for each companion:**
>
> **Aldric:** A) Flank (+1 next attack) | B) Shield Wall — blocks the armoury door (+1 AC, second Baaz cannot pass) | C) Aggressive Strike (1d8+2, takes 1d4)
> **Sera:** A) Scout Shot (1d6 dmg) | B) Mark Target (+2 next attack) | C) Cover Fire (+1 AC for you)
> **Mira:** A) Rush to Aldous — begins healing (stabilize + 1d6+2) | B) Bandage Aldous (stabilize 1 HP) | C) Herbal Boost (+1 save)
> **Serath:** A) Intel (+2 one attack) | B) Dagger from the shadows (1d4+2, target does not see her) | C) Feint (enemy -1 next attack)
> **Lysander:** A) Combat Instruction (+2 attack) | B) Veteran Strike — cleaves into the nearest Baaz (1d10+3) | C) Guard — steps in front of Aldous, takes the next hit
> **Thessaly:** A) Encourage (+1 next roll) | B) Document (+1 ROSE after) | C) Distraction — shouts from the wall, one Baaz turns (skips next attack)
> **Vael:** A) Flanking Shot (1d6 dmg) | B) Honest Assessment (reveals enemy HP) | C) Cover Fire (+1 AC)

> **ABILITY / ITEM USE (choose one, optional):**
> • (Paladin) Cast Bless: +1d4 to attacks and saves for up to 3 targets, Concentration, lasts entire combat. 1 spell slot.
> • (Paladin) Divine Smite: Bonus action after hitting with a melee weapon. 2d8 radiant (+1d8 vs Fiends/Undead). Once per turn. 1 spell slot (or free 1/long rest at level 2+). *The radiant light fills the breach. Aldous sees it. He knows what you are.*
> • (Paladin) Lay on Hands: Heal self or Aldous. Bonus action.
> • (Paladin) Cure Wounds: Heal Aldous 2d8+CHA. 1 spell slot. Replaces attack.
> • (Fighter) Action Surge: Additional Action this round (except Magic). 1/short or long rest.
> • (Fighter) Second Wind: 1d10+[level] HP. Bonus action. 2 uses/long rest, regain 1/short rest.
> • (Any) Drink Potion of Healing: 2d4+2 HP. Bonus action.
> • (Any) Use Bandage on Aldous: Stabilize at 1 HP. Replaces attack.

---

### ENEMY STRIKE — ROUND 1

The Baaz at the armoury door turns its attention to you. It is between you and the interior and it knows it — the position gives it confidence. The scimitar comes fast, a horizontal slash aimed at your midsection.

> **DEFENSE ROLL:** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 14
> **SUCCESS:** Parried. The blade rings off yours.
> **FAILURE:** 1d6+2 slashing damage.
>
> **ALDOUS:** If not healed this round, Aldous takes another hit from the engaged Baaz. He has 1 round remaining before he collapses.

---

### NARRATIVE COMBAT — ROUND 2

The breach dust is settling. The fight has found its rhythm — the ugly, grinding rhythm of combat in a space too small for it. You can hear the garrison alarm spreading through the castle behind you, shouts and running boots, but the reinforcements are not here yet. The south wall is yours to hold.

Aldous is on one knee. His sword is braced against the ground and he is using it like a crutch. The Baaz facing him sees the weakness and grins — they grin, you are learning, in a way that has nothing to do with joy and everything to do with anticipation.

> **ATHLETICS CHECK (optional):** Roll 1d20 + STR modifier | DC 14
> Brace the fallen stone. Narrow the breach. Fewer can get through at once.
> **SUCCESS:** The breach is halved. Wave 2 enters one at a time instead of together. Significant tactical advantage.
> **FAILURE:** The stone shifts but does not hold. The breach remains open.

> **YOUR ATTACK:**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll | DC 13
> Roll 1d20 + your attack bonus.
> **ON HIT:** Roll damage. *If this kills a Baaz: DEATH THROES — it turns to stone. DC 11 STR to free your weapon, or draw backup.*

> **PERCEPTION CHECK (free action):** Roll 1d20 + WIS modifier | DC 13
> **SUCCESS:** You hear scraping on the outer wall. More coming. Round 3. You can prepare.
> **FAILURE:** Wave 2 arrives without warning.

> **COMPANION ACTION — Choose one for each companion:** (same options as Round 1)

> **ABILITY / ITEM USE (choose one, optional):** (same options)

---

### ENEMY STRIKE — ROUND 2

The surviving Baaz commit. Both attack — one high, one low. Coordinated. The draconians fight as a unit and they are better at it than the goblins were. This is not raiding. This is soldiering.

> **DEFENSE ROLL (primary):** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 14
> **SUCCESS:** Blocked. Your training holds.
> **FAILURE:** 1d6+2 slashing damage.
>
> **DEFENSE ROLL (secondary, only if 2 Baaz remain):** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 14
> **SUCCESS:** Deflected.
> **FAILURE:** 1d4+2 claw damage. The second one got through.
>
> **ALDOUS:** If not healed by end of Round 2, Aldous collapses. He is unconscious and begins death saves (3 failures = death, 3 successes = stable at 0 HP). Healing can still save him, but the window is closing.

---

### NARRATIVE COMBAT — ROUND 3 — WAVE 2

**IF BREACH WAS NARROWED:** One Baaz squeezes through the gap. The second is stuck on the other side, trying to find another way. You face 1 new enemy this round.
**IF BREACH IS OPEN:** Two Baaz climb through the rubble simultaneously. You face 2 new enemies.

The second wave is fresh. Unwounded. They have been waiting in the dark while you spent yourself on the first pair, and they know it. The one in front has a notched scimitar and a claw scar across its face — a veteran. It has done this before.

> **INTIMIDATION CHECK (optional, free action):** Roll 1d20 + CHA modifier | DC 12
> **SUCCESS:** You roar. The sound fills the breach. One of the new Baaz hesitates — skips its first attack. The breach is full of Solamnic fury and the draconian was not expecting that.
> **FAILURE:** They are not impressed. They are draconians. They have faced worse than you. (Or they think they have.)

> **YOUR ATTACK — Hold the line.**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll | DC 13
> Roll 1d20 + your attack bonus.
> **ON HIT:** Roll damage.

> **COMPANION ACTION — Choose one for each companion:** (same options)

> **ABILITY / ITEM USE (choose one, optional):** (same options)

---

### ENEMY STRIKE — ROUND 3

The fresh Baaz attacks with the eagerness of something that has been waiting and is now, finally, unleashed. The scimitar comes from above — a chopping blow meant to drive you to your knees.

> **DEFENSE ROLL:** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 15 (fresh enemy, aggressive)
> **SUCCESS:** You catch the blade on yours. Your arms ache. You hold.
> **FAILURE:** 1d6+3 slashing damage. The fresh Baaz hits harder.
>
> **IF SECOND WAVE 2 BAAZ IS PRESENT:** Additional attack.
> **DEFENSE ROLL:** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 14
> **FAILURE:** 1d6+2 additional damage.

---

### NARRATIVE COMBAT — ROUND 4 (FINAL)

The garrison reinforcements are coming — you can hear the boots on stone, the shouted orders, Caeron's voice cutting through the chaos with the precision of a man who has trained for exactly this. But they are not here yet. You have one more round. One more round between the draconians and the interior of Castle Brightholm.

Everything hurts. Your arms are heavy. Your breath is short. The torchlight has the quality of light seen through exhaustion — too bright, slightly unreal. But you are standing. The breach is in front of you and nothing has gotten past.

> **YOUR ATTACK — Last stand.**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll | DC 13
> Roll 1d20 + your attack bonus.
> **ON HIT:** Roll damage. *This is the round that matters. Describe it.*

> **COMPANION ACTION — Choose one for each companion:** (same options)

> **ABILITY / ITEM USE (choose one, optional):** (same options)

---

### ENEMY STRIKE — ROUND 4

The draconians sense the reinforcements too. They fight with desperation now — not the calculated patience of the first round but the vicious last-effort of things that know the window is closing.

> **DEFENSE ROLL:** Roll 1d20 + DEX modifier | DC 15
> **SUCCESS:** You hold. The line holds. The breach holds.
> **FAILURE:** 1d6+3 slashing damage. But you do not fall. You do not step back.

Garrison soldiers arrive. Caeron is at the front. The draconians break — not out of cowardice but out of mathematics. The breach is held. The south wall stands.

---

### AFTER THE FIGHT

The dust settles. The stone Baaz statues steam in the night air. The breach is being filled with rubble and timber by garrison engineers who arrived thirty seconds after the fight ended, which is both impressive and infuriating.

Aldous, if he is alive, is propped against the inner wall. He looks at you. He does not say anything for a long time. Then: 'I will remember this when the Trials come.' He means: you have already passed a trial that no ceremony can replicate.

If Aldous is unconscious, the infirmary team takes him. Mira goes with them, if she is here. The corridor feels emptier.

> **No body search available.** The draconians turned to stone in the breach — the engineers are already building them into the wall. There is a grim poetry to it.

> **NPC GRATITUDE — SER ALDOUS** (if healed)
> Aldous does not pay you. That is not what this is.
> He reaches into his belt and produces a small book — leather-bound, hand-copied, the pages soft with age. *The Rose Commentary.* A treatise on the Measure of the Rose written by a knight whose name you recognize from the chapel histories. Aldous has carried it for thirty years.
>
> 'You have earned this,' he says. 'Not because you fought. Because you chose to heal before you chose to strike.'
>
> **Item gained: The Rose Commentary.** +1 to all Measure checks. +1 ROSE.
> *This is not loot. This is inheritance.*

> **AFTER THE FIGHT — UPDATE YOUR SHEET**
> Record current HP. Mark any used: Second Wind, Action Surge, spell slots,
> Lay on Hands pool, bandages, potions consumed.
> Note if Aldous was healed (affects Scene 60 Trials).
> **Short rest available:** Recover Action Surge, regain 1 Second Wind use. HP: spend Hit Dice.

> **XP:** 15 XP per Baaz (60 total if all 4 killed). Bonus 20 XP if Aldous healed. Bonus 10 XP if breach was narrowed. Bonus 10 XP if Intimidation succeeded.

> **A) The breach is held. Return to the corridors. The night is not over yet.** --> Scene 53_HUB

---


## SCENE 53_SABOTAGE — THE GRAIN STORE FIRE

*Castle Brightholm — Supply Wing, Deep Night*

The smell hits you before the sight does — not woodsmoke, not cooking, but the sharp chemical stink of lamp oil poured on grain. Accelerant. Someone is burning the garrison's food stores on the night before a march, and that is not an accident. That is sabotage.

The supply wing corridor is dark except for the orange glow leaking under the grain store door. You can hear it — the wet crackle of oil-soaked grain catching, and under it, the sound of movement. Footsteps. Not the panicked footsteps of someone who started a fire accidentally. The measured footsteps of people with a job.

You put your hand on the door. It is warm. Not hot yet. The fire is young. Whatever is happening in there, you have minutes, not hours.

**IF SERATH IS IN YOUR PARTY:** They appear beside you. They were already coming — they smelled the oil from the corridor. 'Dragon Army sabotage team,' they say. 'Standard doctrine. Two operatives, civilian clothes, prepositioned inside the target garrison weeks ago. They light the stores the night before the assault.' Their expression is flat. 'I know this because I trained them.'

**IF MIRA IS IN YOUR PARTY:** Mira rounds the corner at a run. 'I smelled the oil from the infirmary. The grain store—' She sees the glow under the door. Her face hardens. That grain store is the one she asked Isak for in Vogler. The one she was going to use for the field hospital. The concept is transferable. 'Those supplies are the garrison's future. If they burn, the march starts hungry.'

> **APPROACH — Choose how to enter:**
>
> **A) Kick the door. Surprise them. Sword drawn.** (+1 SWORD) Proceed to combat immediately. You have surprise — enemies do not act in Round 1.
>
> **B) Stealth. Open the door quietly and assess.** (+1 CROWN)
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Stealth (+2) | DEX | DC 13
> **SUCCESS:** You see them before they see you. Two figures in civilian clothes, one pouring oil on the grain sacks, the other holding a torch. A third — larger, armoured beneath a cloak — stands guard with a hand crossbow. You have one free round of attacks before they react. Proceed to combat with surprise.
> **FAILURE:** The door creaks. The guard turns. The torch drops. Proceed to combat — no surprise for either side.
>
> **C) Sound the alarm first, then enter.** (+1 CROWN, +1 ROSE)
> You shout for the watch. Help will arrive in 3 rounds. The saboteurs hear you and prepare. Proceed to combat — no surprise. Garrison reinforcements arrive after Round 3.

> **COMBAT MODE**
> **Pen & Paper:** Use stat blocks below. Run at your table. Skip to AFTER THE FIGHT.
> **Narrative Mode:** Follow rounds below. Roll when prompted.
>
> **ENEMIES:**
> **Saboteur (2):** AC 11 (civilian clothes), HP 9, Speed 30 ft. Dagger +3 (1d4+1). Oil Flask (thrown, 10 ft): target catches fire, 1d4 fire damage per round until extinguished (action). Desperate: will try to spread fire rather than fight if possible.
> **Dragon Army Infiltrator:** AC 14 (hidden chain shirt under cloak), HP 22, Speed 30 ft. Shortsword +5 (1d6+3). Hand Crossbow +5 (1d6+3, 30/120). Multi-attack: 2 shortsword attacks. Slippery: advantage on saves vs. grapple and restrain. **WILL ATTEMPT TO FLEE if both saboteurs fall.**
>
> **ENVIRONMENT:** The grain store is 30 ft x 20 ft. Grain sacks (half cover). Oil on the floor (5 ft area: DEX DC 12 or fall prone). The fire grows: Round 1 = small (no effect). Round 2 = spreading (disadvantage on Perception from smoke). Round 3 = dangerous (1d4 fire damage per round to anyone within 10 ft of grain sacks). Round 4+ = the grain store is lost.
>
> **OBJECTIVE:** Kill or capture the saboteurs AND extinguish the fire before Round 4.
> **EXTINGUISH:** Athletics DC 13 (smother with cloaks/blankets) or create water (Paladin spell, if available). Replaces your attack that round.

> **ROUND 1 — FIRE AND SHADOW**
>
> *Orange light. Smoke already thickening. The grain sacks are stacked seven high and three of them are burning, the oil turning them into wicks. The saboteurs move with the efficiency of people who have done this before — one pouring, one ready with the torch, the infiltrator turning toward the door with the hand crossbow already rising.*
>
> **YOUR ATTACK:**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll (+5) | DC 14 (Infiltrator AC) or DC 11 (Saboteur AC)
> *Choose your target: the infiltrator is the threat. The saboteurs are spreading the fire.*
>
> **HIT:** Deal weapon damage. If targeting a saboteur: one hit drops them (9 HP, they are not fighters).
>
> **MISS:** Smoke and shadows. The grain store is not an arena — it is a burning room full of obstacles.
>
> **COMPANION ACTION (choose 1):**
> | Companion | Action A | Action B | Action C |
> |-----------|----------|----------|----------|
> | Serath (if present) | Engage infiltrator (+2 attack, they know the training) | Block escape route (infiltrator cannot flee) | Shout Dragon Army command codes (saboteurs hesitate — skip their action) |
> | Mira (if present) | Grab blankets — prepare to smother fire next round | Drag grain sacks from the flames (reduce fire timer by 1 round) | Treat any burn wounds (heal 1d6+2) |
> | Aldric (if present) | Flank (+1 attack) | Shield Wall (+1 AC) | Aggressive Strike (1d8+2, takes 1d4) |
>
> **ENEMY ACTIONS:**
> *Saboteurs:* If not engaged, they pour more oil. Fire advances one round on the timer. If engaged, they fight with daggers (desperate, sloppy, DC 11 defense).
> *Infiltrator:* Hand crossbow at closest target. **Defense roll DC 15.** On hit: 1d6+3 piercing. Then draws shortsword.

> **ROUND 2 — THE FIRE SPREADS**
>
> *Smoke is real now. Your eyes sting. The grain sacks are fully ablaze on the east wall and the heat is pushing you back. You have two rounds before the entire store is lost. The infiltrator is between you and the fire, blade drawn, expression flat — the face of a professional who does not care about the grain or the garrison or anything except completing the mission and getting out alive.*
>
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll (+5) | DC 14 (Infiltrator) or DC 11 (Saboteur)
>
> **IF YOU HAVE NOT STARTED EXTINGUISHING:** The fire advances. One more round.
>
> **OPTIONAL — EXTINGUISH FIRE (replaces attack):**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Athletics (+3) | STR | DC 13
> **SUCCESS:** You smother a section of the fire. The timer pauses. The grain store can still be saved.
> **FAILURE:** The oil reignites. The fire continues to advance.
>
> **INFILTRATOR'S ATTACK:**
> Multi-attack: 2 shortsword strikes.
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Defense roll | DC 15 (first strike)
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Defense roll | DC 15 (second strike)
> Each hit: 1d6+3 piercing. The infiltrator is fast, trained, and does not fight fair.

> **ROUND 3 — DECISIVE MOMENT**
>
> *The east wall is fully ablaze. The smoke is at ceiling level and dropping. Your lungs burn. If the fire is not out by the end of this round, the grain store — and the garrison's food supply for the march — is gone.*
>
> **IF INFILTRATOR STILL STANDING:**
> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Attack roll (+5) | DC 14
> **HIT:** Deal weapon damage. If this drops the infiltrator: they fall. The fight is over.
> **(Paladin) DIVINE SMITE** available: +2d8 radiant. In the firelight, the divine light is almost indistinguishable from the flames. Almost.
> **(Fighter) ACTION SURGE** available: second attack.
>
> **IF FIRE NOT YET EXTINGUISHED:**
> Someone must extinguish it this round or the stores are lost.
> **If you chose option C (sounded alarm):** Garrison soldiers arrive with water buckets. Fire is automatically extinguished. The stores are saved.
> **Otherwise:** Athletics DC 13 (you or a companion).
>
> **INFILTRATOR FLEES (if able):**
> If both saboteurs are down and escape route is not blocked, the infiltrator runs.
> **OPTIONAL PURSUIT:** Athletics DC 14 to catch them. If caught: capture alive (+1 CROWN, intelligence value). If not caught: they escape into the night. Caeron will want to know about this.

> **AFTER THE FIGHT**
>
> **GRAIN STORE SAVED:** The supplies survived. The march starts fed. +2 CROWN. Caeron's assessment of you moves in a direction he does not discuss but you can see in the way he includes you in the next briefing.
>
> **GRAIN STORE LOST:** The supplies are ash. The march starts hungry. All ration costs double for Act 4. Caeron says nothing. His silence is louder than criticism.
>
> **SABOTEURS CAPTURED ALIVE:** +2 CROWN. Under interrogation (Caeron handles this, not you), they reveal the Dragon Army's timeline. The march begins a day earlier. This is an advantage.
>
> **INFILTRATOR CAPTURED ALIVE:** +2 CROWN, +1 SWORD. The infiltrator carries a coded dispatch. Serath, if present, can decode it: the Dragon Army's order of battle for the Vogler assault. This intelligence carries into Act 5.
>
> **IF SERATH USED COMMAND CODES:** +1 CROWN. Serath stands in the smoke-filled grain store and looks at their hands. 'I trained people to do this,' they say. 'Now I am stopping people I trained.' The complexity of this is not lost on them. Or on you.
>
> **IF MIRA DRAGGED GRAIN SACKS:** +1 ROSE. The sacks she saved will become bandage material in Vogler. She already knows this. She has been thinking three steps ahead since the south road.
>
> > **SEARCH THE SABOTEURS (Optional — moral choice)**
> > The saboteurs carry coin and a coded message. The infiltrator's chain shirt is quality steel.
> >
> > **A) Search them.** (No moral penalty — enemy combatants engaged in sabotage against your garrison.)
> > **Loot Roll:** Roll 1d20.
> > 1-5: 1d4 stl. Cheap daggers.
> > 6-10: 2d4 stl. The coded message (intelligence value).
> > 11-14: 3d4 stl. Infiltrator's chain shirt (AC 13, lighter than chain mail).
> > 15-17: 4d4 stl. Chain shirt + a vial of alchemist's fire (2d6 fire, thrown 20ft).
> > 18-19: 5d4 stl. Above + a set of thieves' tools (useful for locked doors in future scenes).
> > 20: 6d4 stl. All above + a Dragon Army officer's signet ring. Serath recognizes it: '*That is a captain's ring. This was not a routine sabotage. Someone important ordered this.*' +1 CROWN.
> >
> > **B) Leave them for the watch.** (+1 CROWN. Proper procedure. Caeron approves.)
>
> **AFTER THE FIGHT — UPDATE YOUR SHEET**
> Record current HP. Mark any used: Second Wind, Action Surge, spell slots, Lay on Hands pool, bandages, potions consumed.
> **Short rest available:** Recover Second Wind, Action Surge.
> **XP:** 10 XP per saboteur (20 total), 20 XP for infiltrator. Bonus 15 XP if grain store saved. Bonus 10 XP if infiltrator captured.

> **A) The grain store is secure. Return to the corridors. The night is not over yet.** --> Scene 53_HUB

---


## SCENE 53_HUB_MORN — THE DAWN BEFORE THE TRIALS

*Castle Brightholm — East Battlements, Pre-Dawn*

You find yourself on the east battlements without entirely deciding to walk here. The sky is the colour of steel being heated — not yet light, but no longer dark. Below, the courtyard is already moving: grooms leading horses, the armourer's apprentice carrying bundles of fletching, a cart being loaded with supplies that say *march* more clearly than any order could.

Three days. Maybe two. And between now and then — the Trials. Caeron has decided to accelerate them. Whatever comes after, you will face it as a sworn squire or not at all.

You lean on the battlement stone. It is cold under your hands. South, beyond the treeline, there is nothing visible — but you know what is there. Two thousand soldiers learning your name the way a river learns a stone: by wearing it down. You are not worn down yet. The bell will ring soon. When it does, the Trials begin.

> **A) Go to the Great Hall. Face the Trials.** --> Scene 60

---


## SCENE 60 — THE ACCELERATED TRIALS

*Castle Brightholm — Great Hall, Dawn*

The day of the Trials begins before dawn. No ceremony — there is no time for it. But someone has lit the chapel candles anyway, all of them, and left them burning without explanation.

Stripped of the usual ritual, the day has a different weight — denser, more honest. Physical evaluation. Combat assessment, Aldric as your opponent. Written Measure examination. An oral panel: Caeron, Aldous, and two senior knights whose names you have never learned because they have been here for thirty years and no longer need names so much as presence.

**IF SERA IS IN YOUR PARTY:** Sera is not in the hall for the Trials — she is on the armoury roof again, where she was the first time you saw her. She watches the sparring bout from above. After, when you pass the armoury, there is a folded note on the step: 'Your footwork gap is fixed. Your guard on the right needs work. I will show you on the road. — S.' This is the most she has ever written to you.

> **ROLL REQUIRED:** Athletics (Sparring Bout) (+3) | STR | DC 15
>
> **SUCCESS (roll 15+):** You disarm Aldric on the third pass. +2 SWORD. The panel leans forward.
>
> **FAILURE (roll 1-14):** Aldric takes the bout. +1 SWORD — they evaluate effort, not only outcome.
>
> *No dice? Flip a coin: Heads = pass | Tails = fail*

> **ROLL REQUIRED:** History / Religion (Written Measure Exam) (+0) | INT | DC 14
>
> **SUCCESS (roll 14+):** Your responses are precise and occasionally surprising. Aldous underlines one answer twice. +2 ROSE. (Paladins: your answer on divine duty is unexpectedly sophisticated.)
>
> **FAILURE (roll 1-13):** Solid, correct, conventional. +1 ROSE.
>
> *No dice? Flip a coin: Heads = pass | Tails = fail*

**Final Oral Question:**
'Name the highest principle of the Solamnic Knighthood.'

> **A) 'Est Sularus oth Mithas. My honour is my life.'** (+2 CROWN) --> Scene 61
>
> **B) 'The protection of the innocent, from which all other laws derive.'** (+3 ROSE) --> Scene 61
>
> **C) 'Courage in the face of darkness, maintained even when the outcome is uncertain.'** (+2 SWORD) --> Scene 61

> **TONIGHT — BEFORE THE OATH**
> The Oath is tomorrow. Tonight is the last night before everything changes. Rest now. After Scene 61, your class-specific subplot (Measure track for Fighters, Dark Gift track for Paladins) will continue.

## PALADIN SCENE P3 — THE TEST

*Castle Brightholm — South Field, Night Before Trials*

> **PALADIN ONLY**
> Fighters: proceed directly to Scene 60.

The south field is empty and dark. You are here because something pulled you — the same wordless pull that brought you to the old chapel. You are getting used to following it. You are not sure this is wise.

There is a figure in the field. Not human — or not entirely. It has the general shape of a person standing very still in the darkness, but the details do not resolve cleanly. It does not threaten. It waits.

It speaks. One question. Simple. Unanswerable by anyone who has not thought about it very carefully:

> **DIVINE SIGN**
> 'You have power that most people in this age do not possess. It came to you through something vast and old that has been watching you since before you knew it was there. The question is not whether you will use it. You will. The question is: for whom?'

The figure waits. It is genuinely asking. This is not a test with a wrong answer — it is a test to see if you have an answer at all, and whether it is yours.

> **A) 'For the innocent. For those who cannot protect themselves.'** Mark 1 tally: PALADINE or MISHAKAL (your choice). (+2 ROSE) --> Scene P3a
>
> **B) 'For those who fight beside me. For the line that holds.'** Mark 1 tally: KIRI-JOLITH. (+2 SWORD) --> Scene P3b
>
> **C) 'For the living things that have no voice in the decisions made about them.'** Mark 1 tally: HABBAKUK. (+1 ROSE, +1 SWORD) --> Scene P3c
>
> **D) 'For the possibility that the world can be better than it is.'** Mark 1 tally: BRANCHALA or PALADINE (your choice). (+2 ROSE) --> Scene P3d
>
> **E) 'I do not know yet. I am still becoming the person who will know.'** Mark nothing. (+1 ROSE, +1 CROWN) --> Scene P3e

---


## PALADIN SCENE P3a — THE TEST — RESPONSE

The figure is still for a long time. Then: 'Good. That answer holds.' It does not say whose answer it is. It does not need to. It was already there when you started speaking.

Award: +2 ROSE. Proceed to Scene 60.

---


## PALADIN SCENE P3b — THE TEST — RESPONSE

The figure's stillness changes quality — something in it settles, like a weapon lowered rather than sheathed. 'That is the answer of a soldier. There is no higher one.' It steps back and is not there anymore.

Award: +2 SWORD. Proceed to Scene 60.

---


## PALADIN SCENE P3c — THE TEST — RESPONSE

The figure turns its head as if listening to something you cannot hear. Then: 'There are more things alive in this world than have names. It is good to remember them.' Warmth. Brief. Gone.

Award: +1 ROSE +1 SWORD. Proceed to Scene 60.

---


## PALADIN SCENE P3d — THE TEST — RESPONSE

The figure makes a sound that might be music if it were louder. 'That is the most difficult answer,' it says. 'It requires you to keep hoping.' A pause. 'Do not stop.'

Award: +2 ROSE. Proceed to Scene 60.

---


## PALADIN SCENE P3e — THE TEST — RESPONSE

The figure is still for a long time. Then, quietly: 'Most people never ask the question. You asked it. That is enough for now.' It is gone when you blink.

Award: +1 ROSE +1 CROWN. Proceed to Scene 60.

---


## SCENE DG3 — THE CROWN

*Castle Brightholm — Night Before the Oath (Paladin Only)*

> **PALADIN ONLY**
> Only triggers if you are LISTENING, COMPROMISED, or FALLEN on the DG track. If you are HELD FIRM throughout: skip to Scene 61 — you will receive your gift there instead.

You are alone in the old chapel. The official ceremony is tomorrow. You have been sitting here for an hour with your hands on your knees trying to remember why you started. The voice does not whisper tonight. It speaks clearly, quietly, with the tone of someone who believes they are offering something genuinely good.

> **DARK TEMPTATION — TAKHISIS SPEAKS PLAINLY**
> Tomorrow they give you an Order. Rose, Sword, Crown — their little hierarchy of virtue. I offer you something they cannot. Not a rank. A purpose. The Dragon Armies will reshape this world. Every Solamnic Knight who rides against them will die for a structure that cannot hold. But a Knight who rides with me — a Knight who carries both edges — could change everything. Not a traitor. A bridge. You know how to hold two truths. I am asking you to hold this one: the light and the dark, working through the same hands.

This is the most sophisticated temptation yet. It is not asking you to be evil. It is asking you to believe the ends justify the means and that you are wise enough to navigate the result. It might even be true. That is what makes it the worst one.

> **A) No. The oath is not a strategy. It is what you are.** (+3 DG: PURIFIED — proceed to DG3_purified) --> Scene DG3_purified
>
> **B) You are tempted — but you pull back. You spend the night in prayer.** (COMPROMISED → LISTENING, LISTENING → HELD, costs you sleep: -2 HP max until long rest) --> Scene DG3_resist
>
> **C) You accept. The bridge metaphor is genuinely compelling.** (FALLEN — proceed to DG3_fall) --> Scene DG3_fall

---


## SCENE DG3_purified — THE PURIFICATION

*Castle Brightholm — Old Chapel, Night Before the Oath*

You say no so clearly that the voice does not just leave — something cleanses. Whatever had been accumulating — the listening, the delay, the compromise — burns off in a single moment of absolute certainty. You know who you are. You know whose you are. Tomorrow the Oath will be the truest thing you have ever said.

> **DG TRACK: PURIFIED ✓✓**
> All previous compromises cleared. Restore any reduced Lay on Hands pool. Restore frozen god tallies — add +1 to highest for this proof of faith. Proceed to DG_GIFT_PURE for your reward.

> **A) Receive your gift.** --> Scene DG_GIFT_PURE

---


## SCENE DG3_resist — THE HARD RETREAT

*Castle Brightholm — Old Chapel, Night Before the Oath*

You pull back. It costs you — not just sleep. The cost is the admission that you were closer than you want to admit. You spend the night in prayer with the specific discomfort of someone who has seen themselves clearly and does not entirely like the view. By morning you are steady. Not clean — steady. That distinction matters. Steady is enough.

> **DG TRACK: PULLED BACK ✓**
> Improved state. Lay on Hands partially restored (+2 to pool). God tallies partially unfrozen. Proceed to DG_GIFT_SCARRED for your reward.

> **A) Receive your gift.** --> Scene DG_GIFT_SCARRED

---


## SCENE DG3_fall — THE BRIDGE ACCEPTED

*Castle Brightholm — Old Chapel, Night Before the Oath*

You have convinced yourself. That is the part that will haunt you later — not that you were deceived but that you did the work yourself. The reasoning was so good. In the morning you take the Oath with the others. The words come out. They feel true. They feel true through something. Through something that is not quite you anymore.

> **DG TRACK: DEEPLY FALLEN ■■■■**
> The Oath is taken. Its power continues to function. The source is no longer what you believe it is. • Lay on Hands heals 1 HP per use until DG4 is resolved. • Divine Smite functions. The radiance is violet-tinged. • Proceed to DG4 — The Reckoning is your next scene on the road to Vogler.

> **A) Continue to Scene 61.** --> Scene 61

---


## SCENE DG_GIFT_PURE — THE GIFT OF STEADFAST FAITH

*Castle Brightholm — After the Oath Ceremony*

After the ceremony, after everyone else has gone, you find something on the chapel step. It was not there when you arrived. There is no note. You do not need one. The warmth in it is unmistakeable — the same warmth from P1, the same quality, made solid and given form. Your god has been watching. Your god is pleased.

> **✦ MAGIC ITEM GAINED: THE UNBROKEN VOW**
> *Wondrous Item (Requires Attunement by a Paladin), Uncommon*
> A silver disc engraved with the words EST SULARUS OTH MITHAS on one side and a five-pointed star on the other. It is warm to the touch and has been since you found it.
> **Mechanics:** While attuned: your Lay on Hands pool increases by 5 HP. Once per long rest: when you or an ally within 10 ft. drops to 0 HP, you may use your reaction to immediately stabilise them and grant them 1 HP. Additionally, you have advantage on saving throws against fear effects.
> **Lore:** Given to a paladin who was tempted and did not bend.

> **✦ MAGIC ITEM GAINED: OATH-KEEPER**
> *Weapon (Longsword), Requires Attunement by a Paladin, Rare*
> A longsword with a blade of white steel and a crossguard shaped like two wings folded in rest. The grip is wrapped in white leather that does not soil. The blade catches light and holds it a moment longer than it should.
> **Mechanics:** +1 bonus to attack and damage rolls. When you hit a fiend or undead, the target takes an extra 1d6 radiant damage. Once per long rest: on a hit, you may choose to maximise the damage rather than rolling. The sword does not glow on command — it glows when it judges the moment worthy.
> **Lore:** Forged in spirit and given form by an act of unbroken faith. In the main campaign, it will glow in the presence of Dragon Army officers who are genuinely conflicted about their service.

> **✦ MAGIC ITEM GAINED: THE VIGIL CLOAK**
> *Wondrous Item (Cloak), Requires Attunement by a Paladin or Knight, Rare*
> A deep blue-grey cloak with a silver clasp shaped like the Solamnic sun. It is heavier than it looks and does not blow in wind.
> **Mechanics:** +1 to AC. Advantage on saving throws against being magically moved or knocked prone. Once per long rest: when an ally within 30 ft. is targeted by an attack, you may use your reaction to impose disadvantage on that attack roll. Cannot be charmed or frightened while in direct sunlight.
> **Lore:** Given to a paladin who stood where they were supposed to stand and did not move.

> **A) Continue to Scene 62.** --> Scene 62

---


## SCENE DG_GIFT_SCARRED — THE GIFT OF THE SCARRED FLAME

*Castle Brightholm or Vogler Road — After Pulling Back*

You do not find it placed with ceremony. It is simply in your hand at some point after — after the hard night of prayer, after the slow return. You are not entirely sure when it arrived.

> **✦ MAGIC ITEM GAINED: THE SCARRED FLAME**
> *Wondrous Item (Requires Attunement by a Paladin), Uncommon*
> A pendant shaped like a flame with a crack through it, sealed with silver. The gold and violet in the metalwork are both deliberately visible — not hidden, acknowledged.
> **Mechanics:** Once per long rest: when you fail a saving throw against a charm or compulsion effect, you may reroll it with advantage. Proficiency in Insight checks when determining if a creature is deceiving you or acting under magical influence. Your Lay on Hands pool is fully restored.
> **Lore:** Given to a paladin who was tempted, bent toward the fall, and pulled back. The scar is not hidden because the gods of good do not hide their histories.

> **A) Proceed to Scene 62.** --> Scene 62

---


## SCENE M3 — TWO OATHS

*Castle Brightholm — Night of the Oath Ceremony (Fighter Only)*

> **FIGHTER ONLY**
> This scene occurs on the night of Scene 61, after the ceremony. Paladins skip to Scene 62.

After the ceremony, after Caeron's sword and the words and Aldous in the corner, you find yourself standing outside the chapel with a very specific question you did not have before you took the oath. The oath says: honour the innocent, obey your commanding officer, serve the Order. But you have now seen, in three weeks of field exercise, two cases where those clauses are in direct conflict. Aldous finds you. Of course he does. 'You have questions,' he says. Not a question.

> **THE MEASURE: THE MEASURE ON CONFLICTING OBLIGATIONS**
> The Oath has three pillars: Rose (justice, compassion, wisdom), Sword (courage, battle, honour), Crown (law, loyalty, duty). The Measure does not rank them. This is intentional. It places the burden of adjudication on the Knight who must live with both the choice and its consequences.

> **A) 'When the three conflict, Rose takes precedence. A law that creates injustice has already broken the Oath.'** (+3 MEASURE TRACK. ROSE orientation) --> Scene M3_rose
>
> **B) 'When the three conflict, Sword takes precedence — the person who holds the line protects the others.'** (+3 MEASURE TRACK. SWORD orientation) --> Scene M3_sword
>
> **C) 'When the three conflict, Crown takes precedence — the structure must hold or nothing else can.'** (+3 MEASURE TRACK. CROWN orientation) --> Scene M3_crown
>
> **D) 'I do not know yet. I think the answer is situational.'** (+2 MEASURE TRACK. BALANCE orientation) --> Scene M3_balance

---


## SCENE M3_rose — THE ROSE PATH

*Chapel Yard*

Aldous looks at you steadily. 'The Rose Knights have always said that. Most of them are right. Some of them have used it to excuse breaking every rule they found inconvenient. The difference is whether you actually know what justice requires or whether you just think you do.' A pause. 'You do. So far.'

> **MEASURE TRACK: ROSE orientation.**

> **A) March at dawn.** --> Scene 62

---


## SCENE M3_sword — THE SWORD PATH

*Chapel Yard*

Aldous considers this. 'The Sword Knights have always said that too. And they are right: the person who does not hold their post creates the hole that everything else falls through. The question is what you do when holding your post requires injustice.' He looks at you. 'You have an answer. I can tell.'

> **MEASURE TRACK: SWORD orientation.**

> **A) March at dawn.** --> Scene 62

---


## SCENE M3_crown — THE CROWN PATH

*Chapel Yard*

'The Crown Knights,' Aldous says. 'The institution has to survive for the ideal to survive — that argument has defended both the best decisions and the worst ones in Solamnic history. The difference is who is doing the reforming and from what motive.' He is quiet. 'You have the motive right. Keep it.'

> **MEASURE TRACK: CROWN orientation.**

> **A) March at dawn.** --> Scene 62

---


## SCENE M3_balance — THE BALANCE PATH

*Chapel Yard*

Aldous is quiet for a long time. Then: 'That is the answer the Measure itself gives, if you read it carefully. The lack of ranking is intentional. It is asking every Knight to do the hardest thing: think. Every time. Even when you are tired.' He nods. 'Harder path. But a real one.'

> **MEASURE TRACK: BALANCE orientation.**

> **A) March at dawn.** --> Scene 62

## SCENE 61 — THE OATH OF SQUIREHOOD

*Castle Brightholm — Chapel, Afternoon*

Caeron's sword is cold on your shoulder. The chapel smells of tallow and old stone and something you will later identify as the specific smell of commitment taking a permanent form. Aldric in the front row, jaw set. Thessaly with her notebook closed. Mira at the back if she is still here. Ser Aldous in the corner.

Caeron speaks the words of the Oath of Squirehood. When you rise, quiet enough for only you: 'Whatever Order claims you — you have earned this.'

> **You Are Now a Squire**
> Total your Order points. The highest score determines which Order claims your oath.

> **LEVEL UP — YOU ARE NOW LEVEL 3**
> **Fighter Level 3:** Full Subclass activates. Champion: Improved Critical (19–20) + Remarkable Athlete (advantage on Initiative and Athletics, move half Speed after critting without provoking). Battle Master: Superiority Dice + Manoeuvres active. Eldritch Knight: Full spellcasting active.
> **Paladin Level 3:** Sacred Oath (Devotion, Ancients, Vengeance, or Glory). Channel Divinity: 2 uses/long rest, regain 1/short rest. Divine Sense is now a Channel Divinity option (bonus action, detect Celestials/Fiends/Undead within 60ft, 10 min). Spell slots increase to 3 first-level.
>
> Native PC — Fighter: HP +7 (total 26). Paladin: HP +7 (total 25).

> **ITEM GIVEN — ALDOUS'S COMPASS**
> A small brass compass, old, with a chip on the case. 'It has been wrong since 862,' he says. 'Points about twelve degrees west of north. I have used it my entire career and navigated correctly every time, because I knew to account for it.'

> **RELATIONSHIP CHECK — ACT 3**
> If you are pursuing **two or more romances**, turn to Scene REST_ROMANCE now before continuing. Resolve that scene, then return here.

> **TONIGHT — AFTER THE OATH**
> The Oath is done. Tomorrow you march south. Tonight is your last night at Brightholm. • FIGHTERS on the Measure track: turn to Scene M3 (Two Oaths) now. M3 leads to Scene 62. • PALADINS on the DG track: turn to Scene DG3 (The Crown) now.

> **A) (Fighter, no Measure track) Rest tonight. March at dawn.** --> Scene 62
>
> **B) (Fighter on Measure track) Seek out Aldous tonight — he said one more conversation.** --> Scene M3
>
> **C) (Paladin on DG track) Tonight, before rest, the voice comes again.** --> Scene DG3
>
> **D) (Paladin, no DG track) Rest tonight. March at dawn.** --> Scene 62
